//RIVER
//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
river

//river c-bet\
when botraisedbeforeflop and not raisesbeforeflop and not calledonflop and not calledonturn and botslastaction = bet
	when random <= 40 bet force

//board states

when straightonboard
	when haveflush raise force
	when havenutstraight raise force
	when others fold force
	
when flushonboard
	when havestraightflush raise force
	when havenutflush raise force
	when have2ndnutflush call force
	when others fold force
	
when fullhouseonboard
	when havequads raise force
	when havefullhouse and havetoppair call force
	when others fold force

when onecardstraightpossible
	when havestraightflush raise force
	when havequads raise force
	when havefullhouse raise force
	when havenutflush raise force
	when haveflush raise force
	when havenutstraight raise force
	when havestraight and (bets = 1 or raises = 1) call force

	when haveset and (bets = 1) call force
	when havetwopair and (bets = 1) call force
	when others fold force

when onecardflushpossible
	when havestraightflush raise force
	when havequads raise force
	when havefullhouse raise force
	when havenutflush raise force
	when haveflush call force
	when others fold force
	
when twopaironboard
	when havequads raise force
	when havefullhouse and havetoppair raise force
	when havefullhouse call force
	when others fold force
	
when tripsonboard
	when havequads raise force
	when havefullhouse and (haveoverpair or havetoppair) raise force
	when havefullhouse call force
	when others fold force

when (board = AKQ or board = KQJ or board = QJT or board = JT9 or board = T98 or 
	board = 987 or board = 876 or board = 765 or board = 654 or board = 543 or
	board = 432) and straightpossible and not onecardstraightpossible
	when havestraightflush raise force
	when havequads raise force
	when havefullhouse raise force
	when havenutflush raise force
	when haveflush raise force
	when havenutstraight raise force
	when havestraight and (bets = 1 or raises <= 2) call force

	when haveset and (bets = 1 or raises = 1) call force
	when havetwopair and (bets = 1 or raises = 1) call force
	when havetoppair and (bets = 1 or raises = 1) call force
	when have2ndtoppair and (bets = 1) call force
	when haveflushdrawand (bets = 1 or raises = 1) call force
	when havestraightdraw and overcards >= 1and (bets = 1 or raises = 1) call force
	when others fold force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
//***********************************First position opponents = 1************************************************************

when position = first and opponents = 1

//***********************************Special Conditions




//flop the nuts
  when havestraightflush and bets = 0 and raises = 0 and (insmallblind or inbigblind) call force
  when havestraightflush and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havestraightflush and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havestraightflush and raises >= 1 raise force
  when havequads and bets = 0 and raises = 0 and (insmallblind or inbigblind) call force
  when havequads and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havequads and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havequads and raises >= 1 raise force
  when havefullhouse and bets = 0 and raises = 0 and (insmallblind or inbigblind) call force
  when havefullhouse and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havefullhouse and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havefullhouse and raises >= 1 raise force
  when havenutflush and bets = 0 and raises = 0 and (insmallblind or inbigblind) call force
  when havenutflush and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havenutflush and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havenutflush and raises >= 1 raise force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  
//flop a flush
  when haveflush and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveflush and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when haveflush and raises >= 1 call force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  
//flop straight and not flushpossible
  when havestraight and not (flushpossible) and bets = 0 and raises = 0 and suitsonboard >= 3 bet force
  when havestraight and not (flushpossible) and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havestraight and not (flushpossible) and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havestraight and not (flushpossible) and raises >= 1 raise force

//flop straight and flushpossible
  when havestraight and flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havestraight and flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when havestraight and flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  
//flop a set and flushpossible
  when haveset and flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveset and flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when haveset and flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//flop a set and an Ace on board
  when haveset and (board = A) and not hand = AA and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveset and (board = A) and not hand = AA and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when haveset and (board = A) and not hand = AA and raises >= 1 raise force

//flop a set and not Ace on board
  when haveset and not (board = A) and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveset and not (board = A) and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when haveset and not (board = A) and raises >= 1 raise force

//flop a set with AA
  when haveset and (board = A) and hand = AA and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveset and (board = A) and hand = AA and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when haveset and (board = A) and hand = AA and raises >= 1 raise force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------  
  
//flop trips and have good kicker not flushpossible
  when havetrips and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and not flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havetrips and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and not flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havetrips and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and not flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//flop trips and not have good kicker not flushpossible
  when havetrips and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and not flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havetrips and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and not flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when havetrips and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and not flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//flop trips and have good kicker flushpossible
  when havetrips and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havetrips and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havetrips and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//flop trips and not have good kicker flushpossible
  when havetrips and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havetrips and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when havetrips and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	
//flop two pair and have top pair and flushpossible
  when havetwopair and havetoppair and flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havetwopair and havetoppair and flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havetwopair and havetoppair and flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//flop two pair and have top pair and not flushpossible
  when havetwopair and havetoppair and not flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havetwopair and havetoppair and not flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havetwopair and havetoppair and not flushpossible and raises >= 1 raise force

//flop two pair and flushpossible	
  when havetwopair and flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havetwopair and flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havetwopair and flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//flop two pair and not flushpossible	
  when havetwopair and not flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havetwopair and not flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havetwopair and not flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  
//flop an overpair and have JJ+ and flushpossible
  when haveoverpair and (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveoverpair and (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when haveoverpair and (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop an overpair and have JJ+ and not flushpossible
  when haveoverpair and (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveoverpair and (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when haveoverpair and (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 raise force

//flop an overpair and not have JJ+ and flushpossible
  when haveoverpair and not (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveoverpair and not (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when haveoverpair and not (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop an overpair and not have JJ+ and not flushpossible
  when haveoverpair and not (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveoverpair and not (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when haveoverpair and not (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop top pair and have A or K and have GK and flushpossible
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and 
	((board = A) or (board = K and not board = A)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and 
	((board = A) or (board = K and not board = A)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and 
	((board = A) or (board = K and not board = A)) and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop top pair and have A or K and have GK and not flushpossible
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and 
	((board = A) or (board = K and not board = A)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and 
	((board = A) or (board = K and not board = A)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and 
	((board = A) or (board = K and not board = A)) and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 raise force

//flop top pair and have A or K and not have GK and flushpossible
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and 
	((board = A) or (board = K and not board = A)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and 
	((board = A) or (board = K and not board = A)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and 
	((board = A) or (board = K and not board = A)) and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop top pair and have A or K and not have GK and not flushpossible
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and 
	((board = A) or (board = K and not board = A)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and 
	((board = A) or (board = K and not board = A)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and 
	((board = A) or (board = K and not board = A)) and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop top pair and have 9-Q and have GK and flushpossible
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible and 
	((hand = Q and board = Q) or (hand = J and board = J) or (hand = T and board = T) or (hand = 9 and board = 9))
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible and 
	((hand = Q and board = Q) or (hand = J and board = J) or (hand = T and board = T) or (hand = 9 and board = 9))
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible and 
	((hand = Q and board = Q) or (hand = J and board = J) or (hand = T and board = T) or (hand = 9 and board = 9))
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop top pair and have 9-Q and have GK and not flushpossible
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible and 
	((hand = Q and board = Q) or (hand = J and board = J) or (hand = T and board = T) or (hand = 9 and board = 9))
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible and 
	((hand = Q and board = Q) or (hand = J and board = J) or (hand = T and board = T) or (hand = 9 and board = 9))
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible and 
	((hand = Q and board = Q) or (hand = J and board = J) or (hand = T and board = T) or (hand = 9 and board = 9))
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop top pair and have 9-Q and not have GK and flushpossible
  when (havetoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible and 
	((hand = Q and board = Q) or (hand = J and board = J) or (hand = T and board = T) or (hand = 9 and board = 9))
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havetoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible and 
	((hand = Q and board = Q) or (hand = J and board = J) or (hand = T and board = T) or (hand = 9 and board = 9))
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when (havetoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible and 
	((hand = Q and board = Q) or (hand = J and board = J) or (hand = T and board = T) or (hand = 9 and board = 9))
	and raises >= 1 call force
	
//flop top pair and have 9-Q and not have GK and not flushpossible
  when (havetoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible and 
	((hand = Q and board = Q) or (hand = J and board = J) or (hand = T and board = T) or (hand = 9 and board = 9))
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havetoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible and 
	((hand = Q and board = Q) or (hand = J and board = J) or (hand = T and board = T) or (hand = 9 and board = 9))
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when (havetoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible and 
	((hand = Q and board = Q) or (hand = J and board = J) or (hand = T and board = T) or (hand = 9 and board = 9))
	and raises >= 1 call force
	
//flop top pair and have GK and flushpossible
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force
  
//flop top pair and have GK and not flushpossible
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop top pair and not have GK and flushpossible
  when (havetoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havetoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havetoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop top pair and not have GK and not flushpossible
  when (havetoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havetoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havetoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force
	
//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

//flop 2nd overpair and have TT+ and board = A
  when have2ndoverpair and (hand = TT or hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK) and (board = A)
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when have2ndoverpair and (hand = TT or hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK) and (board = A)
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when have2ndoverpair and (hand = TT or hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK) and (board = A)
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop 2nd overpair and have TT+ and not board = A
  when have2ndoverpair and (hand = TT or hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK) and not (board = A)
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when have2ndoverpair and (hand = TT or hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK) and not (board = A)
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when have2ndoverpair and (hand = TT or hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK) and not (board = A)
	and raises >= 1 call force

  when have2ndoverpair and board = A and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when have2ndoverpair and board = A and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when have2ndoverpair and board = A and raises >= 1 call force

//flop 2nd overpair and not board = A
  when have2ndoverpair and not board = A and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when have2ndoverpair and not board = A and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when have2ndoverpair and not board = A and raises >= 1 call force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

//flop 2nd top pair and have GK and flushpossible
  when (have2ndtoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (have2ndtoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (have2ndtoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop 2nd top pair and have GK and not flushpossible
  when (have2ndtoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (have2ndtoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when (have2ndtoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force
	
//flop 2nd top pair and not have GK and flushpossible
  when (have2ndtoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (have2ndtoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when (have2ndtoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force
	
//flop 2nd top pair and not have GK and not flushpossible
  when (have2ndtoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (have2ndtoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when (have2ndtoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

//flop pair and not pairinhand and have GK and flushpossible
  when (havepair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havepair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havepair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop pair and not pairinhand and have GK and not flushpossible
  when (havepair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and not flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havepair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and not flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havepair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop pair and not pairinhand and not have GK and flushpossible
  when (havepair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havepair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havepair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop pair and not pairinhand and not have GK and not flushpossible
  when (havepair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and not flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havepair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and not flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havepair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

//overcards = 2 and have AK or AQ or AJ
when overcards = 2 and (hand = AK or hand = AQ or hand = AJ) and bets = 0 and raises = 0 call force
when overcards = 2 and (hand = AK or hand = AQ or hand = AJ) and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
when overcards = 2 and (hand = AK or hand = AQ or hand = AJ) and raises >= 1 fold force

//overcards = 2 and have A or KQ or KJ
when overcards = 2 and (hand = A or hand = KQ or hand = KJ) and bets = 0 and raises = 0 call force
when overcards = 2 and (hand = A or hand = KQ or hand = KJ) and bets = 1 and raises = 0 fold force
when overcards = 2 and (hand = A or hand = KQ or hand = KJ) and raises >= 1 fold force

//overcards >= 1
when overcards >= 1 and bets = 0 and raises = 0 call force
when overcards >= 1 and bets = 1 and raises = 0 fold force
when overcards >= 1 and raises >= 1 fold force

//***********************************First position opponents >= 2************************************************************

when (position = first or position = middle) and opponents >= 2

//***********************************Special Conditions




//flop the nuts
  when havestraightflush and bets = 0 and raises = 0 and (insmallblind or inbigblind) call force
  when havestraightflush and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havestraightflush and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havestraightflush and raises >= 1 raise force
  when havequads and bets = 0 and raises = 0 and (insmallblind or inbigblind) call force
  when havequads and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havequads and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havequads and raises >= 1 raise force
  when havefullhouse and bets = 0 and raises = 0 and (insmallblind or inbigblind) call force
  when havefullhouse and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havefullhouse and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havefullhouse and raises >= 1 raise force
  when havenutflush and bets = 0 and raises = 0 and (insmallblind or inbigblind) call force
  when havenutflush and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havenutflush and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havenutflush and raises >= 1 raise force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  
//flop a flush
  when haveflush and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveflush and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when haveflush and raises >= 1 call force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  
//flop straight and not flushpossible
  when havestraight and not (flushpossible) and bets = 0 and raises = 0 and suitsonboard >= 3 bet force
  when havestraight and not (flushpossible) and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havestraight and not (flushpossible) and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havestraight and not (flushpossible) and raises >= 1 raise force

//flop straight and flushpossible
  when havestraight and flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havestraight and flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when havestraight and flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  
//flop a set and flushpossible
  when haveset and flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveset and flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when haveset and flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//flop a set and an Ace on board
  when haveset and (board = A) and not hand = AA and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveset and (board = A) and not hand = AA and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when haveset and (board = A) and not hand = AA and raises >= 1 raise force

//flop a set and not Ace on board
  when haveset and not (board = A) and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveset and not (board = A) and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when haveset and not (board = A) and raises >= 1 raise force

//flop a set with AA
  when haveset and (board = A) and hand = AA and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveset and (board = A) and hand = AA and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when haveset and (board = A) and hand = AA and raises >= 1 raise force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

	and not flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havetrips and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and not flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

  when havetrips and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and not flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when havetrips and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and not flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//flop trips and have good kicker flushpossible
  when havetrips and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havetrips and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard

  when havetrips and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//flop two pair and have top pair and flushpossible
  when havetwopair and havetoppair and flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havetwopair and havetoppair and flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havetwopair and havetoppair and flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force

	and raises >= 1 call force

  when (havetoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible and

	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible

  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible

  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

	and raises >= 1 call force

	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havetoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop 2nd overpair and have TT+ and board = A
  when have2ndoverpair and (hand = TT or hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK) and (board = A)
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when have2ndoverpair and (hand = TT or hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK) and (board = A)
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when have2ndoverpair and (hand = TT or hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK) and (board = A)
	and raises >= 1 call force

  when have2ndoverpair and (hand = TT or hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK) and not (board = A)
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when have2ndoverpair and (hand = TT or hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK) and not (board = A)
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when have2ndoverpair and (hand = TT or hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK) and not (board = A)
	and raises >= 1 call force

  when have2ndoverpair and board = A and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when have2ndoverpair and board = A and raises >= 1 call force

  when have2ndoverpair and not board = A and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when have2ndoverpair and not board = A and raises >= 1 call force

  when (have2ndtoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

  when (have2ndtoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (have2ndtoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when (have2ndtoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force
	
//flop 2nd top pair and not have GK and flushpossible
  when (have2ndtoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (have2ndtoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible

  when (have2ndtoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

  when (have2ndtoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop pair and not pairinhand and have GK and flushpossible
  when (havepair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havepair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havepair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop pair and not pairinhand and have GK and not flushpossible
  when (havepair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and not flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havepair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and not flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havepair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop pair and not pairinhand and not have GK and flushpossible
  when (havepair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havepair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and flushpossible

  when (havepair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

  when (havepair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and not flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havepair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//overcards = 2 and have AK or AQ or AJ
when overcards = 2 and (hand = AK or hand = AQ or hand = AJ) and bets = 0 and raises = 0 call force
when overcards = 2 and (hand = AK or hand = AQ or hand = AJ) and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
when overcards = 2 and (hand = AK or hand = AQ or hand = AJ) and raises >= 1 fold force

//overcards = 2 and have A or KQ or KJ
when overcards = 2 and (hand = A or hand = KQ or hand = KJ) and bets = 0 and raises = 0 call force
when overcards = 2 and (hand = A or hand = KQ or hand = KJ) and bets = 1 and raises = 0 fold force
when overcards = 2 and (hand = A or hand = KQ or hand = KJ) and raises >= 1 fold force

//overcards >= 1
when overcards >= 1 and bets = 0 and raises = 0 call force
when overcards >= 1 and bets = 1 and raises = 0 fold force
when overcards >= 1 and raises >= 1 fold force

when position = last and opponents = 1

//***********************************Special Conditions




//flop the nuts
  when havestraightflush and bets = 0 and raises = 0 and (insmallblind or inbigblind) call force
  when havestraightflush and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havestraightflush and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havestraightflush and raises >= 1 raise force
  when havequads and bets = 0 and raises = 0 and (insmallblind or inbigblind) call force
  when havequads and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havequads and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havequads and raises >= 1 raise force
  when havefullhouse and bets = 0 and raises = 0 and (insmallblind or inbigblind) call force
  when havefullhouse and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havefullhouse and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havefullhouse and raises >= 1 raise force
  when havenutflush and bets = 0 and raises = 0 and (insmallblind or inbigblind) call force
  when havenutflush and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havenutflush and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havenutflush and raises >= 1 raise force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  
//flop a flush
  when haveflush and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveflush and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when haveflush and raises >= 1 call force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  
//flop straight and not flushpossible
  when havestraight and not (flushpossible) and bets = 0 and raises = 0 and suitsonboard >= 3 bet force
  when havestraight and not (flushpossible) and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havestraight and not (flushpossible) and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havestraight and not (flushpossible) and raises >= 1 raise force

//flop straight and flushpossible
  when havestraight and flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havestraight and flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when havestraight and flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  
//flop a set and flushpossible
  when haveset and flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveset and flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when haveset and flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//flop a set and an Ace on board
  when haveset and (board = A) and not hand = AA and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveset and (board = A) and not hand = AA and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when haveset and (board = A) and not hand = AA and raises >= 1 raise force

//flop a set and not Ace on board
  when haveset and not (board = A) and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveset and not (board = A) and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when haveset and not (board = A) and raises >= 1 raise force

//flop a set with AA
  when haveset and (board = A) and hand = AA and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveset and (board = A) and hand = AA and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when haveset and (board = A) and hand = AA and raises >= 1 raise force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------  
  
//flop trips and have good kicker not flushpossible
  when havetrips and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and not flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havetrips and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and not flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havetrips and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and not flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//flop trips and not have good kicker not flushpossible
  when havetrips and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and not flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havetrips and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and not flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when havetrips and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and not flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//flop trips and have good kicker flushpossible
  when havetrips and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havetrips and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havetrips and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//flop trips and not have good kicker flushpossible
  when havetrips and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havetrips and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when havetrips and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	
//flop two pair and have top pair and flushpossible
  when havetwopair and havetoppair and flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havetwopair and havetoppair and flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havetwopair and havetoppair and flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//flop two pair and have top pair and not flushpossible
  when havetwopair and havetoppair and not flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havetwopair and havetoppair and not flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havetwopair and havetoppair and not flushpossible and raises >= 1 raise force

//flop two pair and flushpossible	
  when havetwopair and flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havetwopair and flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havetwopair and flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//flop two pair and not flushpossible	
  when havetwopair and not flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havetwopair and not flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havetwopair and not flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  
//flop an overpair and have JJ+ and flushpossible
  when haveoverpair and (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveoverpair and (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when haveoverpair and (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop an overpair and have JJ+ and not flushpossible
  when haveoverpair and (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveoverpair and (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when haveoverpair and (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 raise force

//flop an overpair and not have JJ+ and flushpossible
  when haveoverpair and not (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveoverpair and not (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when haveoverpair and not (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop an overpair and not have JJ+ and not flushpossible
  when haveoverpair and not (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveoverpair and not (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when haveoverpair and not (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  
//flop top pair and have A or K and have GK and flushpossible
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and 
	((board = A) or (board = K and not board = A)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and 
	((board = A) or (board = K and not board = A)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and 
	((board = A) or (board = K and not board = A)) and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop top pair and have A or K and have GK and not flushpossible
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and 
	((board = A) or (board = K and not board = A)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and 
	((board = A) or (board = K and not board = A)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and 
	((board = A) or (board = K and not board = A)) and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 raise force

//flop top pair and have A or K and not have GK and flushpossible
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and 
	((board = A) or (board = K and not board = A)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and 
	((board = A) or (board = K and not board = A)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and 
	((board = A) or (board = K and not board = A)) and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop top pair and have A or K and not have GK and not flushpossible
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and 
	((board = A) or (board = K and not board = A)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and 
	((board = A) or (board = K and not board = A)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and 
	((board = A) or (board = K and not board = A)) and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop top pair and have 9-Q and have GK and flushpossible
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible and 
	((hand = Q and board = Q) or (hand = J and board = J) or (hand = T and board = T) or (hand = 9 and board = 9))
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible and 
	((hand = Q and board = Q) or (hand = J and board = J) or (hand = T and board = T) or (hand = 9 and board = 9))
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible and 
	((hand = Q and board = Q) or (hand = J and board = J) or (hand = T and board = T) or (hand = 9 and board = 9))
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop top pair and have 9-Q and have GK and not flushpossible
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible and 
	((hand = Q and board = Q) or (hand = J and board = J) or (hand = T and board = T) or (hand = 9 and board = 9))
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible and 
	((hand = Q and board = Q) or (hand = J and board = J) or (hand = T and board = T) or (hand = 9 and board = 9))
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible and 
	((hand = Q and board = Q) or (hand = J and board = J) or (hand = T and board = T) or (hand = 9 and board = 9))
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop top pair and have 9-Q and not have GK and flushpossible
  when (havetoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible and 
	((hand = Q and board = Q) or (hand = J and board = J) or (hand = T and board = T) or (hand = 9 and board = 9))
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havetoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible and 
	((hand = Q and board = Q) or (hand = J and board = J) or (hand = T and board = T) or (hand = 9 and board = 9))
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when (havetoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible and 
	((hand = Q and board = Q) or (hand = J and board = J) or (hand = T and board = T) or (hand = 9 and board = 9))
	and raises >= 1 call force
	
//flop top pair and have 9-Q and not have GK and not flushpossible
  when (havetoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible and 
	((hand = Q and board = Q) or (hand = J and board = J) or (hand = T and board = T) or (hand = 9 and board = 9))
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havetoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible and 
	((hand = Q and board = Q) or (hand = J and board = J) or (hand = T and board = T) or (hand = 9 and board = 9))
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when (havetoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible and 
	((hand = Q and board = Q) or (hand = J and board = J) or (hand = T and board = T) or (hand = 9 and board = 9))
	and raises >= 1 call force
	
//flop top pair and have GK and flushpossible
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force
  
//flop top pair and have GK and not flushpossible
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop top pair and not have GK and flushpossible
  when (havetoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havetoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havetoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop top pair and not have GK and not flushpossible
  when (havetoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havetoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havetoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force
	
//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

//flop 2nd overpair and have TT+ and board = A
  when have2ndoverpair and (hand = TT or hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK) and (board = A)
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when have2ndoverpair and (hand = TT or hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK) and (board = A)
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when have2ndoverpair and (hand = TT or hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK) and (board = A)
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop 2nd overpair and have TT+ and not board = A
  when have2ndoverpair and (hand = TT or hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK) and not (board = A)
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when have2ndoverpair and (hand = TT or hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK) and not (board = A)
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when have2ndoverpair and (hand = TT or hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK) and not (board = A)
	and raises >= 1 call force
	
//flop 2nd overpair and board = A
  when have2ndoverpair and board = A and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when have2ndoverpair and board = A and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when have2ndoverpair and board = A and raises >= 1 call force

//flop 2nd overpair and not board = A
  when have2ndoverpair and not board = A and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when have2ndoverpair and not board = A and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when have2ndoverpair and not board = A and raises >= 1 call force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

//flop 2nd top pair and have GK and flushpossible
  when (have2ndtoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (have2ndtoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (have2ndtoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop 2nd top pair and have GK and not flushpossible
  when (have2ndtoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (have2ndtoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when (have2ndtoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force
	
//flop 2nd top pair and not have GK and flushpossible
  when (have2ndtoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (have2ndtoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when (have2ndtoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force
	
//flop 2nd top pair and not have GK and not flushpossible
  when (have2ndtoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (have2ndtoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when (have2ndtoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

//flop pair and not pairinhand and have GK and flushpossible
  when (havepair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havepair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havepair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop pair and not pairinhand and have GK and not flushpossible
  when (havepair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and not flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havepair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and not flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havepair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop pair and not pairinhand and not have GK and flushpossible
  when (havepair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havepair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havepair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop pair and not pairinhand and not have GK and not flushpossible
  when (havepair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and not flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havepair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and not flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havepair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

//overcards = 2 and have AK or AQ or AJ
when overcards = 2 and (hand = AK or hand = AQ or hand = AJ) and bets = 0 and raises = 0 call force
when overcards = 2 and (hand = AK or hand = AQ or hand = AJ) and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
when overcards = 2 and (hand = AK or hand = AQ or hand = AJ) and raises >= 1 fold force

//overcards = 2 and have A or KQ or KJ
when overcards = 2 and (hand = A or hand = KQ or hand = KJ) and bets = 0 and raises = 0 call force
when overcards = 2 and (hand = A or hand = KQ or hand = KJ) and bets = 1 and raises = 0 fold force
when overcards = 2 and (hand = A or hand = KQ or hand = KJ) and raises >= 1 fold force

//overcards >= 1
when overcards >= 1 and bets = 0 and raises = 0 call force
when overcards >= 1 and bets = 1 and raises = 0 fold force
when overcards >= 1 and raises >= 1 fold force

//***********************************Last position opponents >= 2************************************************************

when position = Last and opponents >= 2

//***********************************Special Conditions




//flop the nuts
  when havestraightflush and bets = 0 and raises = 0 and (insmallblind or inbigblind) call force
  when havestraightflush and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havestraightflush and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havestraightflush and raises >= 1 raise force
  when havequads and bets = 0 and raises = 0 and (insmallblind or inbigblind) call force
  when havequads and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havequads and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havequads and raises >= 1 raise force
  when havefullhouse and bets = 0 and raises = 0 and (insmallblind or inbigblind) call force
  when havefullhouse and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havefullhouse and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havefullhouse and raises >= 1 raise force
  when havenutflush and bets = 0 and raises = 0 and (insmallblind or inbigblind) call force
  when havenutflush and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havenutflush and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havenutflush and raises >= 1 raise force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  
//flop a flush
  when haveflush and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveflush and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when haveflush and raises >= 1 call force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  
//flop straight and not flushpossible
  when havestraight and not (flushpossible) and bets = 0 and raises = 0 and suitsonboard >= 3 bet force
  when havestraight and not (flushpossible) and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havestraight and not (flushpossible) and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havestraight and not (flushpossible) and raises >= 1 raise force

//flop straight and flushpossible
  when havestraight and flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havestraight and flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when havestraight and flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  
//flop a set and flushpossible
  when haveset and flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveset and flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when haveset and flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//flop a set and an Ace on board
  when haveset and (board = A) and not hand = AA and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveset and (board = A) and not hand = AA and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when haveset and (board = A) and not hand = AA and raises >= 1 raise force

//flop a set and not Ace on board
  when haveset and not (board = A) and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveset and not (board = A) and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when haveset and not (board = A) and raises >= 1 raise force

//flop a set with AA
  when haveset and (board = A) and hand = AA and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveset and (board = A) and hand = AA and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when haveset and (board = A) and hand = AA and raises >= 1 raise force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------  
  
//flop trips and have good kicker not flushpossible
  when havetrips and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and not flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havetrips and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and not flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havetrips and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and not flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//flop trips and not have good kicker not flushpossible
  when havetrips and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and not flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havetrips and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and not flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when havetrips and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and not flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//flop trips and have good kicker flushpossible
  when havetrips and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havetrips and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havetrips and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//flop trips and not have good kicker flushpossible
  when havetrips and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havetrips and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when havetrips and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker) and paironboard
	and flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	
//flop two pair and have top pair and flushpossible
  when havetwopair and havetoppair and flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havetwopair and havetoppair and flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havetwopair and havetoppair and flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//flop two pair and have top pair and not flushpossible
  when havetwopair and havetoppair and not flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havetwopair and havetoppair and not flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havetwopair and havetoppair and not flushpossible and raises >= 1 raise force

//flop two pair and flushpossible	
  when havetwopair and flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havetwopair and flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havetwopair and flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//flop two pair and not flushpossible	
  when havetwopair and not flushpossible and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when havetwopair and not flushpossible and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when havetwopair and not flushpossible and raises >= 1 call force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  
//flop an overpair and have JJ+ and flushpossible
  when haveoverpair and (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveoverpair and (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when haveoverpair and (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop an overpair and have JJ+ and not flushpossible
  when haveoverpair and (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveoverpair and (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when haveoverpair and (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 raise force

//flop an overpair and not have JJ+ and flushpossible
  when haveoverpair and not (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveoverpair and not (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when haveoverpair and not (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop an overpair and not have JJ+ and not flushpossible
  when haveoverpair and not (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when haveoverpair and not (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when haveoverpair and not (hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK or hand = AA) and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
  
//flop top pair and have A or K and have GK and flushpossible
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and 
	((board = A) or (board = K and not board = A)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and 
	((board = A) or (board = K and not board = A)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and 
	((board = A) or (board = K and not board = A)) and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

	and raises >= 1 call force

	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havetoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop 2nd overpair and have TT+ and board = A
  when have2ndoverpair and (hand = TT or hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK) and (board = A)
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when have2ndoverpair and (hand = TT or hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK) and (board = A)
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when have2ndoverpair and (hand = TT or hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK) and (board = A)
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop 2nd overpair and have TT+ and not board = A
  when have2ndoverpair and (hand = TT or hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK) and not (board = A)
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when have2ndoverpair and (hand = TT or hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK) and not (board = A)
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when have2ndoverpair and (hand = TT or hand = JJ or hand = QQ or hand = KK) and not (board = A)
	and raises >= 1 call force
	
//flop 2nd overpair and board = A
  when have2ndoverpair and board = A and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when have2ndoverpair and board = A and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when have2ndoverpair and board = A and raises >= 1 call force

//flop 2nd overpair and not board = A
  when have2ndoverpair and not board = A and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when have2ndoverpair and not board = A and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when have2ndoverpair and not board = A and raises >= 1 call force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

//flop 2nd top pair and have GK and flushpossible
  when (have2ndtoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (have2ndtoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (have2ndtoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop 2nd top pair and have GK and not flushpossible
  when (have2ndtoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (have2ndtoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when (have2ndtoppair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force
	
//flop 2nd top pair and not have GK and flushpossible
  when (have2ndtoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (have2ndtoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when (have2ndtoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force
	
//flop 2nd top pair and not have GK and not flushpossible
  when (have2ndtoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (have2ndtoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 raise force
  when (have2ndtoppair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop pair and not pairinhand and have GK and flushpossible
  when (havepair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havepair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havepair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop pair and not pairinhand and have GK and not flushpossible
  when (havepair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and not flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havepair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and not flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havepair and (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop pair and not pairinhand and not have GK and flushpossible
  when (havepair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havepair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havepair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//flop pair and not pairinhand and not have GK and not flushpossible
  when (havepair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and not flushpossible
	and bets = 0 and raises = 0 bet force
  when (havepair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and not flushpossible
	and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
  when (havepair and not (havebestkicker or have2ndbestkicker or have3rdbestkicker)) and not pairinhand and not flushpossible
	and raises >= 1 call force

//---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

//overcards = 2 and have AK or AQ or AJ
when overcards = 2 and (hand = AK or hand = AQ or hand = AJ) and bets = 0 and raises = 0 call force
when overcards = 2 and (hand = AK or hand = AQ or hand = AJ) and bets = 1 and raises = 0 call force
when overcards = 2 and (hand = AK or hand = AQ or hand = AJ) and raises >= 1 fold force

//overcards = 2 and have A or KQ or KJ
when overcards = 2 and (hand = A or hand = KQ or hand = KJ) and bets = 0 and raises = 0 call force
when overcards = 2 and (hand = A or hand = KQ or hand = KJ) and bets = 1 and raises = 0 fold force
when overcards = 2 and (hand = A or hand = KQ or hand = KJ) and raises >= 1 fold force

//overcards >= 1
when overcards >= 1 and bets = 0 and raises = 0 call force
when overcards >= 1 and bets = 1 and raises = 0 fold force
when overcards >= 1 and raises >= 1 fold force

when others
	when others fold force
